is a board game for two players. It is played on a square board, made of 64 smaller squares, with eight squares on each side. Each player starts with sixteen pieces: eight pawns, two knights, two bishops, two rooks, one queen and one king. The goal of the game is for each player to try and checkmate the king of the opponent. Checkmate is a threat ('check') to the opposing king which no move can stop. It ends the game.\r\nDuring the game the two opponents take turns to move one of their pieces to a different square of the board. One player ('White') has pieces of a light color; the other player ('Black') has pieces of a dark color. There are rules about how pieces move, and about taking the opponent's pieces off the board. Besides, AX-ZIP Extractor is simple and convenient file manager.\r\n\r\nMain Features\r\n\r\nExtraction from ZIP, CAB, RAR, JAR, XAP, GZIP, BZIP2, XZ, TAR and 7Z archives.\r\nExtraction from ISO images (ISO 9660 and ISO 13346 \"UDF\").\r\nSimultaneous work with several archives.\r\nOne drag extraction of files from archive.\r\nSearch of archives and files within the archives.\r\nBookmarks for archives and files in the archives.\r\nSupport of cloud drives and special folders.\r\nSupport of main file manager functions.\r\nSupport of drag and drop technology.\r\nDisplay of archive structure as a tree.\r\nFamiliar Explorer-like user interface.\r\n\r\nOverview\r\n\r\nAX-ZIP Extractor utility views ZIP archives and archives of other types as folders containing folders and files whose structure is shown as a tree.
